			function initialize3605353() {
				var gmap = PF('map' + 3605353 + 'Component').getMap();

				if (true) {
					var nebound = new google.maps.LatLng (0.0, 0.0, true);

				}

				var envistaMapLayers = document.getElementById('mapComponent' + 3605353 + 'Form:mapPanel');
				initMapLayers (envistaMapLayers, gmap, 3605353);
			}

				handleOverlaySelectComplete (xhr, status, args, 3605353, gmap);
				updateDependants(xhr, status, args);
			}

			function updateComponent3605353(xhr, status, args) {
				var gmap = PF('map' + 3605353 + 'Component').getMap();
				if (args.markerId) {
					handleTableSelectionChangeMessage(args.markerId, 3605353, gmap);
				} else {
					var wmap = PF('map' + 3605353 + 'Component');
					handleFilterChangeMessage(args, 3605353, wmap);
				}

			}
